<br/><span style="display:none;" id="data/plumed-nest/nspe/plumed.datpb">The PBMETAD action with label <b>pb</b> calculates the following quantities:<table  align="center" frame="void" width="95%" cellpadding="5%"><tr><td width="5%"><b> Quantity </b>  </td><td><b> Description </b> </td></tr><tr><td width="5%">pb.bias</td><td>the instantaneous value of the bias potential</td></tr></table></span><div class="tooltip" style="color:green">PRINT<div class="right">Print quantities to a file. <a href="https://www.plumed.org/doc-master/user-doc/html/_p_r_i_n_t.html" style="color:green">More details</a><i></i></div></div> <div class="tooltip">ARG<div class="right">the input for this action is the scalar output from one or more other actions<i></i></div></div> <div class="tooltip">STRIDE<div class="right"> the frequency with which the quantities of interest should be output<i></i></div></div>=1000 <div class="tooltip">FILE<div class="right">the name of the file on which to output these quantities<i></i></div></div>=COLVAR
